< review>
I love all the Hangar 18 gyms! This one is bouldering only, which is great for me. It's so nice to have variety in the IE when it comes to climbing. Sometimes they have events, which is super fun. Their prices are so much better than other gyms in southern California. Right now, membership is only $36 a month! It's a terrific workout, and bouldering has helped get me in the best shape of my life. And... It's fun for big kids too.< /review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
This place is great. It's hidden away in the industrial area of the city. Parking is readily available even when it's busy.

Whenever I go to this gym it's hardly ever busy and that's great. The people I see eat the gym are regulars. Everyone is nice and encouraging they help you when you are stuck on a problem.

When the gym is busy there's still enough space to have a great time.

The staff at this gym is the best always friendly and helpful.</text>

< text>
I had my brows microbladed last week and I love them. Victoria is an expert and a true artist. I was nervous committing
to something semi-permanent and all I can say is I should have gone sooner.

My appointment was at 10:30 AM and the first 30 mins was just the consult.  She evaluates the face and bones in order
to ensure the correct shape and placement.  I'm in love with how she accentuated my brow bones with the brow shape
and gave me an instant eye lift.

I appreciated the drawing period where she drew in the ideal brow and then negotiated length according to my comfort
level and how bold I was willing to go.  She also tested the colors next to my hair to ensure I was satisfied with the
shades.  She measured twice then cut once.  Victoria makes you feel so comfortable.  I did not feel a thing during the
appointment.  A little stinging afterwards, but very minor.

I'm very particular about my face. For my profession I work on faces and mouths all day and I am detail oriented to a
fault sometimes and I would go as far as sometimes hard to please. I can genuinely say she went above and beyond my
brow goals!  I have already recommended her to some of my coworkers.</text>

< Text>
I've always had very sparse eyebrows with little definition. I'd been curious about microblading but didn't know anyone who'd had the procedure done. Based on the Yelp reviews and ratings, I decided to try with Victoria. The procedure itself was far less painful than I had envisioned, maybe the first cuts hurt a bit, but as soon as the numbing cream went on it was bearable, and I might mention I have a rather low pain tolerance. I will say despite being told that the procedure wasn't truly finished until I'd had the touch up session, I did panic initially, and thought I was quite unhappy with how it had turned out. In time, possibly after a month, they finally took their current shape and I'm very happy with how they look even pre - touch up. So, essentially, totally worth it! Makes getting ready way easier, but do be patient if they dont look exactly as you hoped in the first few weeks, once they heal they'll be perfect!< /Text>

< Review>
So my  1991 jeep that i had driven for 15 years and put over 120k miles on had started running rough and it finally stalled and would not start.  I had it towed to Wayne and sons to be diagnosed.   This vehicle gave an ignition code of 24 (crankshaft position sensor) and it was in a crank no spark condition.  They told me after a day or so that the computer was bad on the vehicle and that a new computer would cost $1000.00 plus installation, plus the 250 bucks they had already spent on the diagnosis.  I asked if I could get a computer somewhere else  ( due to the high cost) and have them install it.  (At the time i did not know the install was 4 screws about 5 minutes of labor)  they said I could get a computer and they would install it.  I bought a brand new one from Orilleys and delivered it to them.  They spent half the day and then told me the new computer from Orilleys was defective and that they see bad parts from them all the time.  But they had to spend more time to diagnose my vehicle after they got the new defective computer so the total was now over 500 bucks plus the 250 I spent on the computer at Orilleys.  Luckily for me Orilleys took the part back and refunded me my money.    I had replaced the following parts on the vehicle before I brought it to Wayne and sons.  Crankshaft position sensor, maps sensor, and coil.  I had my vehicle towed back to my home.  I put in a new starter and the situation was the same.  I had the old computer in the vehicle rebuilt and the situation and code were the same code 24 and still a crank no spark.  I decided to sell the vehicle for 500 bucks and a guy came with his test light and figured out there was spark above the coil.  I had seen on YouTube that the older jeeps will not restart unless you unplug the crankshaft position sensor for 5 minutes and then plug it back in.  We put the old coil into the vehicle and after leaving the crankshaft sensor unplugged for 5 minutes the vehicle started up and in 20 minutes was running perfectly.  I suspect Wayne and sons did not know to unplug the crank sensor for five minutes and there is even the possibility that they neglected to test for spark above the coil.  In either case the code was the same 24 when i dropped the vehicle of to them as it was when i picked it up and after I installed the rebuilt computer.  I now suspect the new computer I bought was fine from Orilleys, but because Wayne and sons could not figure it out they needed to have an answer.   For 15 years this car gave me great service and the guy from craigslist who fixed it in 30 minutes and bought it for 500 bucks now has a good running dependable 4x4 no thanks to Wayne and sons.   They deserve a negative rating but I will have to settle for 1 star.< /Review>
